  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

  <span id="freeText1938431257604363650" style="display:none">Fate isn't something to mess with and now, neither is Alex. <br /><br />Alex has always feared two things: losing herself in the Awakening and being placed on the Elixir. But love has always been stronger than Fate, and Aiden St. Delphi is willing to make war on the gods—and Alex herself—to bring her back. <br /><br />The gods have killed thousands and could destroy entire cities in their quest to stop Seth from taking Alex's power and becoming the all-powerful God Killer. But breaking Alex's connection to Seth isn't the only problem. There are a few pesky little loopholes in the whole an Apollyon can't be killed theory, and the only person who might know how to stop the destruction has been dead for centuries. <br /><br />Finding their way past the barriers that guard the Underworld, searching for one soul among countless millions, and then somehow returning will be hard enough. Alex might be able to keep Seth from becoming the God Killer or she might become the God Killer herself.</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<div class='spoiler'>
This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    She does love him but not in the same way she loves Aiden I think. It is more of the kind of love she feels for her friends but it is deepened by the <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    She does love him but not in the same way she loves Aiden I think. It is more of the kind of love she feels for her friends but it is deepened by the connection they share. She does think he is redeemable at some point and she does explain how she really feels about him later on. <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>

<div id="review_245269202" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/245269202" />
    <a title="Kayleigh {K-Books}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3996633-kayleigh-k-books"><img alt="Kayleigh {K-Books}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540157695p2/3996633.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/245269202?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kayleigh {K-Books}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kayleigh {K-Books}" href="/user/show/3996633-kayleigh-k-books">Kayleigh {K-Books}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3996633-kayleigh-k-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer245269202" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer602102644438966639"><a href='http://k-booksxo.blogspot.co.uk/2013/04/blog-tour-apollyon-covenant-4.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Apollyon Review on K-Books</a><br/><br/><b>
  <u>**Please Note: Contains Spoilers for Deity and Elixir.</u>
</b><br/><br/>Oh. My. Freaking. Gods! There are no words in this universe that could explain my feelings about this book. I went through so many emotions throughout this book, from freaking out, to crying to laughing and hopeful. I just loved every single second of it and it is without a doubt my favourite book of all time.<br/><br/>Alex has connected with Seth. Unaware of her previous state of mind and her feelings for Aiden, Alex know</span>
  <span id="freeText602102644438966639" style="display:none"><a href="http://k-booksxo.blogspot.co.uk/2013/04/blog-tour-apollyon-covenant-4.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Apollyon Review on K-Books</a><br /><br /><b>
  <u>**Please Note: Contains Spoilers for Deity and Elixir.</u>
</b><br /><br />Oh. My. Freaking. Gods! There are no words in this universe that could explain my feelings about this book. I went through so many emotions throughout this book, from freaking out, to crying to laughing and hopeful. I just loved every single second of it and it is without a doubt my favourite book of all time.<br /><br />Alex has connected with Seth. Unaware of her previous state of mind and her feelings for Aiden, Alex knows only one thing. Seth is her other half and she needs him. Aiden is determined to bring the real Alex back and won't give up on her. But Aiden is still reeling from the fact that he had to put her on the Elixir. If Alex comes back will she ever forgive him for doing the one thing he promised not to? And will they have the strength to defeat Seth and Lucian and stop a war with the Gods from happening? One this is for certain... they are at war now and not everyone is going to survive!<br /><br />It's fair to say that I have been dying for this book for a long time. I absolutely love it and the ending of both Deity and Elixir had my dying for more and needed to know what happened to these characters next. This is without a doubt the best book in the series so far. One thing I adore about this series is that you never know what is going to happen next. The books just get better and better the furthur through the series you get. It's just phenomenal. One thing Jennifer is brilliant at is throwing you twists and turns that you would never see coming. As soon as I was sure I knew what was coming and what was going to happen she would throw something in there where I was left like: *gasp* No way... I never saw that coming! I was literally left on the edge of my seat all the way through the book, freaking out and quite frankly scared to finish the book as I didn't want it to ever end and I just knew Jennifer would throw something in there that would leave me speechless and dying for Sentinel.<br /><br />I don't want to say too much about the characters as I don't want to spoil anything but Apollyon was the only book where I wanted to smack Alex... HARD! I know I know it's not her fault, she's connected to Seth and doesn't really have control over what she was doing. But oh my gods I just wanted someone to smack her so damn hard and knock some damn sense into her. Everytime Seth was inside her head talking to her through the connection I found myself screaming "GET OUT OF HER HEAD" at the book. YES... this book turned me crazy!!<br /><br />Aiden... Oh just when I thought I couldn't possibly love him any more. I just love him. He's perfect and all the way through reading I just kept sending Jennifer messages saying, Why can't he be real? He is and will always be my number one book boyfriend of all time because he is just amazing and perfect. You really see how amazing and loyal he is, how he will never give up on Alex even if he has to fight Gods for her. What I really loved about Aiden was that in Apollyon you really see a more vulnerable side to him. In the first 3 installments of the series you really see the strong Aiden who is fighting his growing feelings for Alex and trying to train her to be the best Sentinel she can be. In Elixir, which is from Aiden's POV, we do see a new side of him but he's still fierce, loyal and protective. However in Apollyon you see the vulnerability in him and how his actions in Elixir affected him and how he feels guilty about what he did. I really loved seeing that side of him.<br /><br />Now I won't talk about Seth all that much as I'm pretty sure everyone knows how I feel about Seth by now. At the end of Deity I hated Seth... I mean physically hated him where I wanted to jump in the book and kill him myself! In Elixir... yep continued to hate him and I was convinced I would forever hate him. By the end of Apollyon I no longer hate him... don't get me wrong I still do not like him AT ALL but I can't hate him. He has done some questionable things and I don't think he should get away with them as he is guilty of causing hundreds of people to be killed. BUT I feel really sorry for him. It is so obvious that all he wants is acceptance and to be loved. Seth has never really had that and he thinks he has found that with Lucian. It is obvious (to me anyway) that Seth is just being manipulated and used by Lucian for his own gain and I feel so sorry for him that he can't see that. Though at the same time I wanna punch him and say WAKE UP STOP BEING AN IDIOT! I am really looking forward to seeing what happens with Seth in the next installment of The Covenant series.<br /><br />Overall this is without a doubt the best Covenant book so far but there is no doubt in my mind that Sentinel will surpass it. Every Jennifer L Armentrout book I read just enforces my belief that she can do no wrong. She is a writing goddess and there is nothing she can write that I won't love and obsess over. Apollyon is no different, it is without a doubt my favourite book of Jennifers, and of all time in fact but there is no doubt in my mind that whatever book she comes out with next, will it be the next Covenant novel, Lux novel or something else it will blow my mind.<br /><br />I am dying to read Sentinel and find out how it all ends but at the same time I am heartbroken that there is only one book left. How can we be nearly finished with this series and what on earth am I to do then? I will just have to cry in a corner... or just re-read the books over and over again.<br />Apollyon is such a fast and amazing roller-coaster ride that will have you bouncing with happiness one minute and freaking out the next. With so many twists and turns you might end up with whiplash this is one book that is not to be missed. I am left hanging on to every word and dying for the next book. Definitely a must-read for everyone! This is one series that is not to be missed out on. Jennifer is officially the queen of writing and I will forever be waiting and dying for her next novel.</span>
  <a data-text-id="602102644438966639" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7305102975307257457">i want to begin with the bone i have to pick with JLA. this is the first time im actually really mad at her. <br/><br/>the point of a novella is an additional story. its presence (or absence) should have no effect on the overall arc of the main series. its a nice little bonus. if there is important information that is necessary to have before beginning the next book in the series, IT SHOULD BE INCLUDED IN A MAIN BOOK!!! how am i expected to (logically) begin this immediately after the previous book and ju</span>
  <span id="freeText7305102975307257457" style="display:none">i want to begin with the bone i have to pick with JLA. this is the first time im actually really mad at her. <br /><br />the point of a novella is an additional story. its presence (or absence) should have no effect on the overall arc of the main series. its a nice little bonus. if there is important information that is necessary to have before beginning the next book in the series, IT SHOULD BE INCLUDED IN A MAIN BOOK!!! how am i expected to (logically) begin this immediately after the previous book and just be okay with a massive chunk of the story missing!?!?? i had to read several chapters before i realised i personally didnt forget something that happened, i just had never read it to begin with. its extremely frustrating and ensures that my reading experience begins with an negative start. im really disappointed she did this.<br /><br />that being said, once i got over my initial anger and could somewhat piece together the information i was missing, i did enjoy this. i love how the gods are becoming bigger players in the story after being absent at the beginning of the series. this does definitely feel like a filler book, as not much really happens other than forming a plan for the upcoming war. i do have a feeling the next book is going to be an epic conclusion to this series though.<br /><br /><b>↠ <i>3.5 stars</i></b></span>

Like a cobra striking, I took Aiden’s legs out from under him and he was on his back before another breath could be taken. Straddling him, I placed my hands on his shoulders. The marks of the Apollyon glowed a vibrant blue and raced over my skin. I leaned in, placing my lips above his and the words that came out of my mouth were mine… but weren’t. “All moments end, Saint Delphi. And now yours has.” I pressed my lips to the corner of his and he flinched. “You are weak because you love.” Aiden stared up at me, unblinking. “To love is not weak. Love is the strongest thing there is.” My lips curved into a smile. There is the way the body curls into itself when it wants death. There is the silent scream for release. There are the eyes, and they speak even when the tongue no longer works. And then there is the soul that rots so poorly when death is wanted but withheld that it carries a certain stench.” Ice shot through my veins, turning my blood to slush. At that moment I knew no matter how much I fought, this… this was going to suck.<br /><br /><i>* this i thinks is Extra from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9761771.Pure__Covenant___2_" title="Pure (Covenant, #2) by Jennifer L. It was pretty epic.<br />A bolt of white light flew from Thanatos’ hand and there wasn’t a single thing in this world that could move fast enough. Not even Seth, I was betting.<br />It hit me just below the chest and my legs collapsed from underneath me. Red-hot, searing pain sliced through my skin and my face smacked off the ground. I didn’t even feel it. There was nothing but the razing pain locking up my muscles.<br />God bolts sucked.<br />Aiden yelled my name, and then I thought I heard my name called again, but it was inside my head, loud, and so very angry… and it sounded like Seth.<br />Without any warning, the ground trembled under my twitching body. A flash of golden light cascaded through the clearing. Warmth stole over my body. Weakly, I lifted my head.<br />Two leather-clad legs stood before me.<br />“That is enough, Thanatos.” Apollo’s voice was calm, but it was that creepy, deadly calm I never wanted to be on the receiving end of.<br />“N-n-nice of y-you to s-show up,” I gasped.<br />“Shut up, Alex.” Apollo strode forward. A ray of light followed his steps.<br /><br /><a href="http://twishort.com/pvEcc" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #4:</a><br />“They do.” Apollo’s eyes narrowed on me. “But I was hoping there was something knocking around in her brain that held the answer to that little problem. But—” Apollo smacked a hand down on my leg. “Must you always be moving some part of your body?”<br />I glared at him as I not-so-gently removed his hand. The contact of his flesh on mine brought the marks of Apollyon out like nothing else. And I knew he saw them by the way his eyes darted over my face. “It’s not hurting you,” I said.<br />“It’s annoying.”<br />“You’re annoying,” I shot back.<br /><br /><br /><i>

  <u>Update (27.12.2012):</u>
</i><br /><a href="http://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/312425568859012" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #7:</a><br />Absolute power—unforgiving and hard, pure as it was deadly— coursed over my skin. I reared back, summoning the fifth and final element. Intense blue light erupted from my palm.<br />Akasha ripped from me, arcing through the air like cloud-to-cloud lightning, homing in on its target and striking true. The sky crackled and heated. One second, the automaton was on his knee, and the next he was nothing but a pile of shimmery dust.<br />“Good gods,” came Olivia’s hoarse whisper.<br />Another automaton took the fallen one’s place, swinging out with a metal hand that clinked and clicked. Fire sparked from its open mouth. I spun, catching the broad side of his arm and twisting. The hoarse shout of pain was lost in the clash of metal, the thunder of bullets finding another automaton.<br />It raised its bull face and snapped at me with massive jaws. “Please.” I placed my hand on the massive forehead.<br />Blue light coursed over the head and down the body, lightening up the metallic skull and bone structure. For a moment, it was like a pretty x-ray or a jellyfish—a really disturbing jellyfish—and then cobalt light radiated from its eyes and open mouth. It imploded—caved in on itself, turning to nothing but dust.<br />And then the crap really hit the fan.<br />The automatons—every last one of the freaky bull things—turned on me. They moved quickly, metal legs rattling and clinking. Fire spewed from their mouths like the poor man’s version of a dragon. They came from all directions, Apollyon-seeking missiles with “Kill Alex” stamped all over them.<br />Fire came from them, blinding and intense. Nothing existed outside the flames. No sound. No sight. My world was red and orange...<br />And my world was tinted in amber.<br />Alex? His voice came through the thrumming connection.<br />I ignored him and the way his consciousness slid in alongside mine. What are you up to?<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <u>Update (26.01.2013):</u>
</i><br /><a href="http://twishort.com/hKOcc" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #8:</a><br />"Sounds like a smart idea." Dark humor laced Aiden's voice. "You might want to get your gun off my brother's face while you're at it."<br /><br /><a href="http://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=323159137785655&amp;set=a.286761674758735.51175.285190961582473&amp;type=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #9:</a><br />There was a knock, and we drew apart an instant before the door swung open and Deacon's mop of head popped in. Aiden groaned, but his eyes lightened up several shades.<br />"Good morning!" Too much cheer ring in his voice for this time of the morning.<br />My cheeks burned as i mumbled, "Morning."<br />Before either of us can say another word, Deacon darted from the door and launched him self on the bed, soaring through the air like a human projectile. I jerked to the side with the split-second to spare. He landed with his legs on his brother and the upper part of his body between us.<br />Deacon threw his arms behind his head, folding them as he tipped his head beck and greened at us. "it's like puppy pile."</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer361322826" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4001862763807635180">HOLY DAIMON BABIES. Jennifer has done it again! <br/><br/>Apollyon is even better than the previous in the series, and will leave you wishing you already had the next one on your e-reader waiting for you. I kid you not, I jerked back and clicked back and forth hoping I was wrong and hadn't reached the end yet. I for real pouted for a good ten minutes. But, Jennifer has a way of writing endings that make you crave her next book without hating her for leaving it the way she did, and I LOVE her for that!<br/><br/>In A</span>
  <span id="freeText4001862763807635180" style="display:none">HOLY DAIMON BABIES. Jennifer has done it again! <br /><br />Apollyon is even better than the previous in the series, and will leave you wishing you already had the next one on your e-reader waiting for you. I kid you not, I jerked back and clicked back and forth hoping I was wrong and hadn't reached the end yet. I for real pouted for a good ten minutes. But, Jennifer has a way of writing endings that make you crave her next book without hating her for leaving it the way she did, and I LOVE her for that!<br /><br />In Apollyon we get to see SO many changes in the group of Alex's friends that we love. And a great change in Alex. There's a lot of growth and maturity in the group, and my favorite is watching Aiden really begin to open up and step up. Oh Aiden...I do love me some Aiden.... *sigh*<br /><br />unfortunately, with how things ended in #3 and #3.5, I can't say too much about the changes in the group without giving certain things away. But trust me, this is a MUST. READ. <br /><br />Apollyon will blow you away, have you gasping, your heart clenching...and racing (sheww, you will definitely need to fan yourself a few times) and overall have you on the edge of your seat waiting to see what happens on the next page.<br /><br />Honest to God, it was amazing and I can't wait to see what happens next!<br /><br />I was given an ARC to read and give my honest review. </span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14102859197611761972"><u>
  <b>Do you ever just stop and think of all the different ways you'd love to <s>torture</s> <i>murder</i> a character?</b>
</u><br/><br/>Because that's all I'm thinking of right now. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602647296ra/30234892.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Oh and how could anyone have waited <b>
  <i>so long</i>
</b> for the last book?!?!<br/><br/>This is a <b>re-read</b> and yet all I want to do is ignore writing this review and go onto the next book even though <b><i>I know</i> how it all ends</b>.......ahhh I'm not looking forward to that.😓<br/><br/>And I swear, I feel like I'm repeating the same thing over and over again in each review xD. Just me ram</span>
  <span id="freeText14102859197611761972" style="display:none"><u>
  <b>Do you ever just stop and think of all the different ways you'd love to <s>torture</s> <i>murder</i> a character?</b>
</u><br><br>Because that's all I'm thinking of right now. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602647296ra/30234892.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Oh and how could anyone have waited <b>
  <i>so long</i>
</b> for the last book?!?!<br><br>This is a <b>re-read</b> and yet all I want to do is ignore writing this review and go onto the next book even though <b><i>I know</i> how it all ends</b>.......ahhh I'm not looking forward to that.😓<br><br>And I swear, I feel like I'm repeating the same thing over and over again in each review xD. Just me rambling on and on about how much I love these guys—but I just can't stop.😍<br><br><b>
  <u>🛑WARNING: SPOILERS FROM PREVIOUS BOOKS!!!🛑</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“To love is not weak. Love is the strongest thing there is.”</b>
</blockquote><br><b>Aiden St. Delphi</b> does it again.🥺 He refuses to give up on Evil-Alex even after Normal-Alex has connected to the Seth and being told that there was no hope for her. Agghhhh Aiden &amp; Alex!!! <b>Their love for each other makes me want to cry.😭😍</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602728946ra/30239068.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Omg Alex's Apollyon powers were <b>✨A M A Z I N G✨</b> And there's so much growth in her, even Laadan mentions how mature Alex has become (although I mean, that's bound to happen when you've dealt with the things she has😬). <b>STILL. MY FAVOURITE WAS ALEX GOING APOLLYON ON ALL THOSE SUCKERS.😈😆</b> <i>(Apollyons really are OP xD)</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602729359ra/30239092.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>We see wayyy more of <b>Deacon, Luke, Olivia, Marcus,</b> and yes, <b>even Lea</b>. I love how Marcus and Alex's relationship have improved <b>A LOT</b> since the first book. It almost looks like they were never hostile towards each other xD. <br><br>And <b>NOW</b> is when Marcus actually acts like Alex's uncle and talks about the sleeping arrangements between the her and Aiden.😂😂😂 That's funny lol. At least he's doing his duty as her guardian lol.<br><br>Now <b>DEACON</b>.😍😍😍<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1596503552ra/29912531.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gosh, why are the <b>St. Delphis</b> just so lovable?!?! I would 100% love having a spin-off of Deacon, but I know that's never going to happen <i>(or maybe it's the "never to say never" thingy)</i>. <br><br>From the first book, he was seen as the laid-back and drunk addict teen, who didn't seem to care at all about anything or what his brother thought, but oh how wrong that was. <b>Deacon</b> fiercely loves Aiden and wants more than anything for him to be happy. The comments he makes whenever he's around Aiden &amp; Alex, too hehe.😏🥰<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Skittles?"<br><br>"Please."<br><br>I dumped some into his open palm, then picked out the green ones. Aiden grinned at me.<br><br>"You know I don't like the green ones?"<br><br>Shrugging, I popped them in my mouth.<br><br>"The few times I've seen you eat them, you leave the green ones behind."<br><br>Deacon popped his head between our seats.<br><br>"That's true love right there."<br><br>"That it is."</b>
</blockquote><br>^ I love this guy. &lt;3<br><br>Also, there were a lot of references to (a show? I'm pretty sure) <b>Supernatural</b> and even though I totally haven't watched it, I love how JLA adds in these kind of reference to real-life tv shows xD.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Go ahead," Apollo said to Luke. "Tell them what it is, since it's obviously hugging material."<br>Crimson stained Luke's cheeks. "Legend goes that one of the gates to hell is in Stull Cemetery in Kansas."<br>"Oh, gods," I muttered, remembering where I'd heard this before. "Wasn't that a season finale on Supernatural?" When the boys nodded, my eyes rolled. "Seriously? Are Sam and Dean going to be there?”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Ahh yes, and <b>Apollo</b>. The guy known to pop in at the worst time and scare the hell out of the others😂. I mean, if a God just poofed in out of nowhere, I'd be pretty freaked out , too xD <i>(he obviously enjoys doing that)</i>. LOL and whenever he appeared, almost always something funny would come out of it.😆<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“They do.” Apollo’s eyes narrowed on me. “But I was hoping there was something knocking around in her brain that held the answer to that little problem. But—”<br><br>Apollo smacked a hand down on my leg. “Must you always be moving some part of your body?”<br><br>I glared at him as I not-so-gently removed his hand. The contact of his flesh on mine brought the marks of Apollyon out like nothing else. And I knew he saw them by the way his eyes darted over my face. “It’s not hurting you,” I said.<br><br>“It’s annoying.”<br><br>“You’re annoying,” I shot back.<br><br>To our left, Aiden rolled his eyes. “All right, children, back to the important stuff.”</b>
</blockquote><br>Aghhh that twist at the end, though.......the first time I read this book I <b>NEVER</b> thought of it being <i>
  <b>him</b>
</i> all along. But, when you think about it.....it's so obvious.😂 What can I say? I'm always <b>terrible</b> at guessing who the culprit is. <s>And now is that time when I <b>really, <i>really, </i></b>wish I could jump in a book and kill someone in the most creative ways possible. (Yes, I might be a little crazy)</s><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602730836ra/30239149.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There are many things I want, but one thing I <b>definitely <i>don't want</i> is FOR THIS SERIES TO END <s>AGAIN</s></b>😭😭😭 <br><br>Well, I guess I should be preparing my <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13605723.Sentinel__Covenant___5_" title="Sentinel (Covenant, #5) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Sentinel</a>
</b> box of tissues..........<br><br><pre>
  <b>“Eíste pánta mou…”<br>"You are my everything.”</b>

Jennifer's writing is absolutely superb (there was no doubt) and I loved this book as much as the others, but unlike Deity, I didn't end this book feeling like I had just licked a battery or that someone stole my favorite toy.<br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/1718494/why-is-the-rum-gone.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400356ra/775663.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com" title="rum gone" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br>(or bottle of rum as it was....hehe)<br><br>It's funny, Apollyon was probably just as much action-packed if not more than its predecessors in the Covenant Series, but at the last page, I was left with that feeling you get before a big storm strikes. I grew up in Tornado Alley, and if you have experienced the absolute stillness in the air before a tornado hits, you know the sensation I'm talking about. Why is that strange do you ask? Considering all the intense, gory action that led up to the last few pages....well you will know when you read it, just know it is intense and a little heart-wrenching altogether hence why I'm confused that I was able to put down the book in such a calm manner.<br><br>One thing that kept bothering me throughout the story was a disturbing out-of-body dream/vision Alex has in the book that left me feeling unsettled through the remainder of the story....I mean the possibility of the story ending so tragically....it hurts....I MEAN HOW THE F*** WAS I SUPPOSED TO CONCENTRATE ON AIDEN &amp; ALEX'S BEAUTIFUL LOVE WITH THIS IMPENDING DOOM THREATENING TO TAKE AWAY MY HEA!!!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400356i/775664.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="screaming" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>....deep breaths....<br><br><br>The meat &amp; potatoes of this book really came down to the mental and emotional struggle between Seth and Alex's bond. Redemption or not? Forgiveness or hate? Understanding or love? Alex had to find the strength within herself in order to come out the other end of the tunnel ready to lead her people into war. Sometimes I hated Seth. Sometimes I felt sorry for him. Mostly, I think he needs to put on his big boy pants; life is tough and you can't decimate the world because mommy didn't love you enough (harsh, but I don't take it back). Yes....there is that bit of him being addicted to akasha and drunk on the power, but I'm talking brass tacks people! Seth is bambi and a douche canoe all boxed up like a McDonalds Happy Meal. We will just have to wait and see if Alex is able to turn the lights on at home or if the house will stay dark in Sentinel. <br><br>In a lot of ways, this book was a bridge to prepare readers for what I'm sure will be a very epic and emotional ending (of which I have no doubt Jennifer will be bringing in all the big guns). Most people hate filler books. I know. But this is not a filler book. I think that's a derogatory connotation to how great this book was, it's the last leg of the journey to the battlefield (?). It's intense, there is baggage...lots and lots of emotional baggage to be dealt with. And it's sad. I may have sniveled a little into a tissue a time or three. There were so many lingering questions up to this point in the series and Apollyon gave me a lot of the answers to ideas and theories I had been tossing around in my head.<br><br>Aiden.<br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/i%27ve%20never%20been%20more%20aroused" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400356ra/775665.gif" alt="i've never been more aroused photo: I've never been more aroused.... Iveneverbeenmorearoused.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Holy wet undies. <br><br>So I don't think I can elaborate any further without giving away key pieces in the story. It's a journey of knowledge, emotion, and hopefully the final steps to the temple of OH MY GOD EPIC ENDINGS. I know I was a fat man sweatin in a cake shop below waiting for this release, but I have to admit that I'm content at the moment to wait on the edge of the cliff and overlook the scenery before I take the plunge into Sentinel. Read it. Love it. <br><br><br><br>O.M.G....I have set an alarm on my iphone and requested the day off work in anticipation for Apollyon, I absolutely cannot frickin wait! Jennifer Armentrout is a writing Goddess.....<br><br>G O D D E S S. <br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/gifs%20love%20you" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398752ra/770926.gif" alt="gifs love you photo: love you frez loveyoufrez.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am sweatin like a fat man in a cake shop waiting for this book release :))) </span>
  <a data-text-id="2441140838380091272" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_235020987" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/235020987" />
    <a title="Jana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4033116-jana"><img alt="Jana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590925674p2/4033116.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/235020987?book_show_action=true">Nov 13, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jana" href="/user/show/4033116-jana">Jana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4033116-jana?shelf=blog-reviewed">blog-reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4033116-jana?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4033116-jana?shelf=jennifer-l-armentrout">jennifer-l-armentrout</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4033116-jana?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer235020987" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2097792354922523659"><br/><br/>You know when I said that DEITY was the best Covenant book and I didn't know how anything could top it, well now I'm just eating my words because APOLLYON oh my gosh just pushed DEITY into a faraway place never to be seen again. Ha. But seriously, just when you think something is JLA's best work, another book of hers get released and then THAT becomes her best work. I don't know how she does it but wow I'm so proud of my favourite author. *bows* <br/><br/><br/>I've always been such a fan of Greek Mythology and</span>
  <span id="freeText2097792354922523659" style="display:none"><br /><br />You know when I said that DEITY was the best Covenant book and I didn't know how anything could top it, well now I'm just eating my words because APOLLYON oh my gosh just pushed DEITY into a faraway place never to be seen again. Ha. But seriously, just when you think something is JLA's best work, another book of hers get released and then THAT becomes her best work. I don't know how she does it but wow I'm so proud of my favourite author. *bows* <br /><br /><br />I've always been such a fan of Greek Mythology and I love how JLA incorporated that into the story. We see and meet a lot more gods in APOLLYON (YES!) and I hope to see a lot more in the last book! Can't get enough of the gods, yo!<br /><br /><br />ALEX! I seriously adored Alex in this book. If you've read my past reviews of the first three books, I found Alex a really annoying, indecisive, spoiled brat but in APOLLYON, she matures and makes (usually) the right choices. For me, what she lacked in the previous books totally makes up for in this. She's loyal, snarky, has a really big heart, and selfless. She always thinks of others. Not to mention her narration is frigging hilarious. <br /><br /><br />WHOA. I need a cold shower after this. The romance between Alex and Aiden really steps up and oh my gosh do we get some sexy scenes!! The Underworld scenes *DIES* Those two are at it like rabbits! LOL not that I was complaining. Anyway, their love for each even grows and just when you think you couldn't fall in love with Aiden a little bit more, you do. I'll be honest here, Aiden has never been my top JLA boy and probably never will be, but now I can see why a LOT of people love him. With APOLLYON, he shows us different sides to him that we don't know and it was just refreshing to see. <br /><br /><br />We all know I hate Seth, right? Yes I do and I was so goddamn happy when I was reading a book and Seth was barely in it. Like, just a tiny little bit. I know a lot of readers think there's still hope for him and redemption, but to be honest I just want to kick his ass. HATE HIM. <br /><br /><br />I will cry so much in the last book since I just can't imagine letting go of this cast of characters. Alex, Aiden, Deacon, Luke, Apollo and everyone I just can't bear to not read about them again. I know they're not all going to survive the next book but *sniff* I'm just hoping. I loved reading about them working as a group and like they're a family. And Marcus, I love ya dude!!<br /><br /><br />Obviously this wouldn't be a JLA novel without non-stop action, suprising twists and secrets. When the enemy was revealed, my mouth was hanging open. I was like WHAAAAA?? How did I not guess that?!? Maybe coz I was so distracted by Aiden but yeah, if you look hard enough, there are some hints but I thought it was all wonderfully done. And there was literally non-stop action, I was so worried for them that my heart was beating so fast haha. <br /><br /><br />There's so many of my favourite scenes that take place - where they meet the special someone, the Alex and Ladaan scenes, but the Underworld scenes are probably my favourite one, and I can honestly say this is the best Covenant book so far in my opinion and no doubt that Sentinel will be even better. Jennifer just keeps getting better with each book in the series! <br /><br /><br />This book will no doubt make you laugh (hey, this is JLA after all), giggle uncontrollably, swoooooon and of course, there are also touching scenes that will make you cry. My favourite author ever Jennifer L. Armentrout is the queen of YA (and NA and Adult) and she is slowly taking over the publishing world. You'd be crazy not to read any of her books. :) <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2097792354922523659" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_584864982" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/584864982" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/584864982?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=cheesy">cheesy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=decent-secondary-characters">decent-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=martyr-heroine">martyr-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=insufferable-mary-sue-heroine">insufferable-mary-sue-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=life-is-hard">life-is-hard</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=die-heroine-die">die-heroine-die</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=heroine-is-a-cow">heroine-is-a-cow</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring-main-characters">boring-main-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=emo-hero">emo-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer584864982" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10509565232399050255"><b>Spoilers</b><br/><br/>This was pretty much what I expected… It wasn't good, it wasn't awful… Okay, it was pretty awful but it wasn't the worst thing I've ever read — there were loads of cheesy parts, predictable arcs and nonsensical dialogue… But I have to admit there was the occasional somewhat entertaining moment.<br/><br/>Why do I keep reading this series?<br/><br/>1. I like (most) of the secondary characters.<br/>2. It reminds me of Vampire Academy, which I love (mostly, sort of).<br/>3. Once I start a series I find it hard to give up</span>
  <span id="freeText10509565232399050255" style="display:none"><b>Spoilers</b><br /><br />This was pretty much what I expected… It wasn't good, it wasn't awful… Okay, it was pretty awful but it wasn't the worst thing I've ever read — there were loads of cheesy parts, predictable arcs and nonsensical dialogue… But I have to admit there was the occasional somewhat entertaining moment.<br /><br />Why do I keep reading this series?<br /><br />1. I like (most) of the secondary characters.<br />2. It reminds me of Vampire Academy, which I love (mostly, sort of).<br />3. Once I start a series I find it hard to give up even when I know it'll be rubbish.<br /><br />The worse thing about the series is the protagonist, Alex. She is one <b>boring</b> bitch. Even when she shows her dick-head side, she's still boring as fuck. <br /><br /><b>Other thoughts</b><br /><br />-I was excited to see 'Evil Alex' because there wasn't enough of her in <i>Elixir</i>. Unfortunately 'Evil Alex' wasn't evil AT ALL. <br />Does she kill anyone? No. Does she hurt anyone enough to cause long term damage? No. Does she say anything vile? No, she's just slightly more snarkier and bitchier than usual. It was a disappointment.<br />I couldn't take 'Evil Alex' seriously when she kept referring to Seth as 'My Seth'. It was weird. I'm guessing it was meant to show that Alex felt possessive and protective of Seth but it sounded lame… And it reminded me of how a parent refers to their child in conversation. The whole 'My Seth' thing came across as rather incestuous. <br />Another disappointment and somewhat of a cop out was the fact that Alex and Seth never met whilst they were bonded… Instead JLA took the easy route and conveniently had them hundreds of miles apart because it was easier to write. What a waste. It would have been great to see Seth and Alex all over each other, that at least would have caused major angst and drama between Alex and Aiden, and it would have breathed life into the lame love triangle. Is it even a love triangle when it's obvious that Alex only wants Aiden? <br />It's disappointing that JLA wrote the Seth/Alex bond + the effects of the bond so simply, and without imagination and daring. The previous three books built up this idea of a crazy-ridiculous-strong-impossible-to-break-unique bond yet it wasn't any of those things… All it did was make Alex more insufferable and more easily influenced by Seth… It was anticlimactic and it came across as silly and it was made even sillier when the bond was broken easily, and after a mere few chapters. How did it break? Through the power of twu wuv — it was corny and cheesy and made me sick.<br /><br />-Alex had the personality of a dead frog in other words she was a Mary Sure. I honestly couldn't figure out what her appeal was. Why did Aiden love her? <br />Her voice was beyond annoying — her one liners were utter rubbish and I HATED the amount of times she said butt or crap - I wish she'd swear properly or not all, I was sick of her swearing like some dorky tween from the 80's.<br />Alex was so up herself — she thought everything was about her and that the gang were risking their lives for her benefit. The only reason anyone was protecting her was because it was for their own interest, but big headed Alex couldn't get that through her thick head… Even when she was told several times that the gang weren't helping her for her but for themselves she still thought it was all for her. Ugh.<br /><br />-I've never liked Alex, she's like every other paranormal YA heroine. Well, actually she isn't, she's worse because she used to be a BULLY. She used to bully Lea as a child and she made everyone gang up on her, torment her and she even spat on her! <br />Why wasn't this mentioned in previous books? 1. Because Alex has never given a fuck about Lea 2. Alex never thought she did anything wrong by bullying Lea 3. Alex thinks she's perfect 4. Alex hates Lea and thinks she isn't worthy of a second thought unless of course she's 'slut shaming' her or being a bitch to her and 5. Alex is a self centered, horrible, nasty piece of work.<br />Alex had somewhat of an epiphany in this book and realised maybe her being a BULLYING BITCH was sort of bad. Does she feel guilty for tormenting Lea for no fucking reason? No, she just feels sort of sheepish about it. Did she give Lea an apology for bullying her as a child because she was jealous? No. She thought there would be no point. WTF?! Alex called her names, isolated her, made everyone gang up on her and spat on her and she doesn't think that was worth an apology?! <br />Yet <i>she</i> still held a grudge against her uncle Marcus because he was somewhat distant towards her growing up… And she wanted an apology and explanation for him treating her like that even though what he did to Alex was NOTHING in comparison to what Alex did to Lea. How did Alex not see her own hypocrisy and double standard? How did Alex not realise that if Marcus's lukewarm attitude hurt her than her own HOSTILE attitude towards Lea, hurt Lea??! WHAT A BITCH. ALEX IS A VILE FUCKING WANKER BITCH!<br />What's even worse is that in all the other books Alex acted like Lea was the bitch, that Lea was the unreasonable one, that Lea was the horrible person and that Lea was the one who started their antagonistic relationship. Alex never once made out that Lea's dislike of Alex was due to the bullying she suffered at Alex's hands. And then on top of that Alex goes around acting all goody-goody and self righteous and nice when in actual fact she's a DISGUSTING COW. <br />I could have handled reading about a heroine who was a bully, I would have actually found said heroine interesting and maybe even sympathetic and likeable if it was handled right but I can't even begin to warm to a bullying heroine that 1. Acts likes she's done no wrong and is perfect, warm and loving person and 2. Can't be bothered to apologise or at least act remorseful. Ugh.<br />Alex is a BITCH. The true heroine of the series is Lea… Of course, JLA had to kill her off because she hates strong non-virginal females. <br /><br />-I hated how Alex thought Seth could be redeemed — he murdered thousands of people and was responsible for a fucking apocalypse! There's no redeeming that — just because he had a less than happy childhood doesn't excuse what he did. Most people have something shit in their lives, that in no way means that it's a-okay if they go around starting apocalypses and murdering thousands of innocents! Seth isn't redeemable, he's a murderer and he played a part in bringing about the end of the world… It doesn't matter if his mummy didn't love him! He's still a psychopath!<br />Oh, it gets even worse, the thick cow thinks she's 'failed Seth'. It doesn't seem to cross Alex's mind that 1. No-one forced Seth to become a psychotic murderer, he chose to and 2. She's not his bloody mum, he's not her FUCKING responsibility, she's only known him a few bastard months! Yet the dumb bitch still thinks it's all her fault that he's a hateful power hungry psycho. She's so dumb.<br /><br />-I'm liking Aiden more, he's still bland and cliched but I did find his love for Alex quite sweet.<br /><br />-Most of the side characters are good. They're not the most layered or unique of characters but they are pretty entertaining - Lea, Olivia, Marcus, Caleb… I thought they were decent enough.<br /><br />-Why do all the immortal gods sound like a cross between a wannabe gangster and a dorky tween?<br /><br />-Caleb appearing in ghost form to help Alex just reminded me of Mason/Rose in VA. I hate how much of the series is picked straight out of VA.<br /><br />-I got tired of the amount of times Aiden's eyes and jaw were mentioned. I want to read a story not various fucking descriptions of Aiden's body parts!<br /><br />-I'm sick of heroines looking in the mirror and noticing some profound change in their appearance because of all the shit they've been through. It's so cheesy and it's just a lazy way of trying to say that the heroine has changed/become deeper without putting any actual effort in developing the heroine in a way that the reader can see for themselves instead of being told in some convenient, inorganic and nonsensical fashion.<br /><br />-I wasn't impressed with the depiction and handling of the secondary female characters. They were all written in a way to make Alex look better than all the <i>other girls</i>.<br />Lea was made out to be a shallow harpy then was killed off. Olivia was just the grieving girlfriend and was barely in it. Ladaan was a pathetic damsel in distress who had been pining for a man for decades even though said man was in love with her friend. Ugh. I wish authors would be brave and talented enough to write amazing side female characters who had their own struggles and victories instead of them being used as props to make the heroine seem speshul.<br /><br />-Please don't tell me Alex is pregnant. That was the hint I got towards the end… I hope I'm wrong. I mean, what's with all the teen pregnancy in YA?<br /><br />Yea, Alex was shit. <br />I'll be reading the next one but I won't be starting any new future series by JLA. Her books are all the same… Boring Virginal Mary Sue meets Mysterious Manslut Sexy Guy… Manslut treats Mary Sue like shit… Mary Sue is speshul snowflake and will save the world or some shit… Manslut wuvs Mary Sue because she's virginal… Mary Sue whines, moans, acts dumb and somehow manages to save everyone… Manslut and Mary Sue commit to each other for life even though they're only teenagers. UGH. <br />I can't wait for the <i>Covenant</i> and <i>Lux</i> series to finish… I've had enough. I wish I didn't feel the need to finish every series I start because its torture reading books I know will be rubbish. I shall persevere though, I always do.<br /><br /><br /><b>ETA 14/4/13. I just remembered some other rubbish.</b><br /><br />-Where the fuck was the storyline? The first half was just Alex moaning about Seth and the bond and the second half was her moaning about how shit her life was. And why the fuck didn't we get to see the build up and beginnings of the apocalypse for ourselves? Instead we had Aiden and the gang casually tell Alex that the world had gone to fuck since she'd been locked up. Was it too much effort to actually write it happening first hand?<br /><br />-What the fuck was with all the mentions of tv shows (Supernatural, Charmed…) and other books? Any time Sam or Dean or Harry Potter was mentioned it took me right out of the story.<br /><br />-Worst of all she mentioned her <i>Lux</i> series and had a character swoon over the guy on the front cover. Was I meant to find that cute or funny? It was pathetic and sad.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10509565232399050255" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12149734678593895044">Just give me a second to take this all in......<br/><br/><a href='http://gifsoup.com/view/996843/britney-spears-crying.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412748ra/811796.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='http://gifsoup.com' title='GIFSoup' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>GIFSoup</a><br/><br/><br/>Okay, now onto the review which won't contain any spoilers at all(I hope). First off can I say she has done it again! JLA is the only author I've known that can grab your heart with every word and just rip it out with an ending!!! Apollyon was definitely the quiet before the storm.....Sentinel is going to be CRAZY!!!! To insure spoiler safety I will talk about the character that we all LOVE!!!!!<br/><br/><br/><b>Aiden:</b> Aiden........HOLY DAIMON BUTT YOU ARE</span>
  <span id="freeText12149734678593895044" style="display:none">Just give me a second to take this all in......<br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/996843/britney-spears-crying.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412748ra/811796.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><br><br>Okay, now onto the review which won't contain any spoilers at all(I hope). First off can I say she has done it again! JLA is the only author I've known that can grab your heart with every word and just rip it out with an ending!!! Apollyon was definitely the quiet before the storm.....Sentinel is going to be CRAZY!!!! To insure spoiler safety I will talk about the character that we all LOVE!!!!!<br><br><br><b>Aiden:</b> Aiden........HOLY DAIMON BUTT YOU ARE THE HOTTEST SENTINEL ALIVE!!!!!!!! Throughout the whole book I couldn't stop saying "Oh Aiden!!!" I seriously love you and you are everything I want in a book boyfriend!!!! Aiden did not disappoint in this book he came through hard and strong and I loved that so much! Alex is a lucky girl to have someone that understands her crazy ways and loves her more than anything. Yes, I know I was #TeamSeth for awhile but Seth cannot compete with Aiden at all!! #TeamAiden FOR LIFE!!!!<br><br><br><b>Alex:</b> I really loved how much Alex has grown throughout this series, she is way more mature in this book and has put her bitch fits to the side......well not the whole time lol and that is why I love her! Even though Alex has grown she is still not afraid to speak her mind and kick ass if she has to, I mean come on she is the Apollyon she can do anything she wants.Being the Apollyon isn't all that easy. Alex must accept her fate and fight against it at the same time in order to save the world....Alex literally has the weight of the world on her shoulders and I'm hoping she makes it through.<br><br><br><b>Seth:</b> YOU SO DAMN EVILLLLLLL!!!!! I had so much faith in you and now I don't know what to think anymore *sigh* what has come over you???? What happened to the fun loving Seth I've grown to love? I am so DONE with you for now!<br><br><br><b>Apollo:</b> YOU ARE WONDERFUL!!!!! I really enjoyed Apollo in this book, he looked out for Alex in his own crazy way and I'm glad Alex has someone like him to look out for her when she needs it the most. I hope to see more of him in Sentinel!<br><br><br><b>Romance:</b> A SHIT LOAD OF IT!!! HOLY GODS YOU WILL NOT BELIEVE ALL THE SEX/LOVE SCENES WITH ALEX AND AIDEN!!!! CAN WE SAY HOTTT DAMN!!!! This book is what everyone has been waiting for for along time and I am really happy that Alex and Aiden aren't afraid to show affection and let others know their in love. This book was so romantic on so many levels I still can't wrap my head around it, I LOVED THIS BOOK!!!<br><br><br><b>Action:</b> Not so much which is fine with me, I'd rather have more Alex and Aiden love scenes any day.<br><br><br><b>Plot:</b> GREAT as always of course!<br><br><br><b>Overall:</b> Best book in the series to build up for Sentinel and I cannot wait!!!!! I so wish they were giving out ARCS for this one because I would kill for it(not really)! I am really sad this series has to come to an end so soon I really feel like I started reading this series yesterday and it is one of those books you cannot get out of your head and you think about it constantly...ugh so bittersweet!!! *tear*<br><br><br><b>Top Five Reasons Why You Should Read Apollyon:</b><br><br>1. Aiden.....need I say more<br><br>2. Hott love scenes #YUM<br><br>3. Akasha butt kicking<br><br>4. Someone doesn't make it(well that's is not a good reason)<br><br>5. A terrifying Visit from the God of War and you wont believe who it is!<br><br><br><b>Rating:</b> Apollyon Good!<br><br><br>Alice <a href="http://www.rottenapplereads.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">@RottenAppleReads</a></span>

<div id="review_1059130066" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1059130066" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1059130066?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016776453" href="/book/show/17735125-apollyon">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1059130066" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7603232308777243262"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n0a7j09qTZ1snlqo0o1_400_zps8201d8f3.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411340219ra/11217190.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_n0a7j09qTZ1snlqo0o1_400_zps8201d8f3.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Apollyon is book #4 in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. <br/><br/>There are advantages and disadvantages to binge reading an entire series from start to finish. The advantages, especially for those of us who might be slightly memory deficient, is to not have to wait that pesky year between books and then not be able to remember what happened in the previous book. The disadvantage, is that I am so immersed into this world, into these characters, that I am pretty much worthless as a contribut</span>
  <span id="freeText7603232308777243262" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n0a7j09qTZ1snlqo0o1_400_zps8201d8f3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411340219ra/11217190.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n0a7j09qTZ1snlqo0o1_400_zps8201d8f3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Apollyon is book #4 in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. <br><br>There are advantages and disadvantages to binge reading an entire series from start to finish. The advantages, especially for those of us who might be slightly memory deficient, is to not have to wait that pesky year between books and then not be able to remember what happened in the previous book. The disadvantage, is that I am so immersed into this world, into these characters, that I am pretty much worthless as a contributing member of society otherwise. I am pretty much living these books, whether I am actually reading nor not. I think about little else. I’m not sure if this is normal or not. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/potion_zps8bedb983.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411340219i/11217191.jpg" alt=" photo potion_zps8bedb983.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Alex has awakened. The problem is that she immediately connected to Seth. Everything she feared, happened. She lost herself. Aiden never gave up. First they tried the Elixir but he knew it was wrong. This was not the way to bring Alex back. So he locked her back up and just talked to her. All day every day, reminding her how much he loved her. In the end, the rose necklace around her neck, the symbol of the love Aiden has for her, is what saved her.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/rosenecklace_zps8556b1f6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411148303i/11198050.jpg" alt=" photo rosenecklace_zps8556b1f6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“Something so small had been the one thing to break the connection. But it wasn’t the rose itself, but what it symbolized—Aiden’s love for me and how I felt for him—something pure and natural, an emotion not forced.”</i>
</b><br><br>Aiden and Alex have gone public with their love. They figured that the pure/half relationship problem was the least of their worries. They and their little band of friends and family have got to find a way to stop Seth and Lucian. But there is a God that is helping Seth and Lucian. One God that wants all of the power. So the other Gods have decided that since Alex has broken her connection with Seth, they will support her. They want Seth and Lucian stopped. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/apollo_zps1a28c04a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411340219i/11217192.jpg" alt=" photo apollo_zps1a28c04a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Alex needs to find out how she can steal the power from Seth before he takes it from her. With Apollo’s help, she and Lucian have to go to the underworld to find a past Apollyon that holds this information. But it is said that those that travel to the underworld never return. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_m5tosbKGqS1qe2f2qo1_500_zps4fa75a8e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399758944i/9592842._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_m5tosbKGqS1qe2f2qo1_500_zps4fa75a8e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>And what if they do get this information and she drains Seth’s power? Then she would be the God killer. What happens then? <br><br><b>
  <i>“Gods, I was so not old enough or mature enough to be making these kinds of decisions.”</i>
</b><br><br>Our group travels from Illinois to the underworld to South Dakota and to Olympus itself. Alex is broken and put back together again, both physically and emotionally. I remember in one of the previous reviews I complained that there wasn’t enough of the love story yet. Well, that is so not the case anymore. The love story between Alex and Aiden is epic. I could highlight quotes all day and just fill up the review with them. Their love for each other is epic, sigh worthy, swoon worthy, do I need to go on? <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/olympus_zps221e1f6c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411340219i/11217193.jpg" alt=" photo olympus_zps221e1f6c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>And need I remind you that Alex JUST turned 18. She has the fate of the entire world, billions of people, on her shoulders. This book of course, ended on a cliff hanger but that’s fine. It’s fine because I am immediately going into the final book. This is something I need to do to retain my own sanity. So I will close with a couple of quotes. Stay tuned for the conclusion to this epic series. I can’t wait to find out how it all ends.<br><br><b>
  <i>“So this is the Apollyon?”<br>“That would be me.”<br>“For some reason, I expected you to be taller.”<br><br>“To love is not weak. Love is the strongest thing there is.”<br><br>“Eiste panta mou…”<br>You are my everything.”</i>
</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7603232308777243262" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25293586-sandra-ladygrey-reads?shelf=half-stars-needed">half-stars-needed</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1358035914" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2528624796716828526"><b>“Whatever you do, don't break my brother's heart. You are his world. And if you leave it, it will destroy him.”</b><br/><br/><b>Actual rating: 4.3 out of 5 stars</b><br/><br/>The thing about this series is that every book gets better and better and better. I loved 80% of this book so much and enjoyed the other 20% a lot. There's action, romance and a lot of sassy remarks that really does not make this the ideal book to read while on a train because you will start laughing all of a sudden and have people staring at you.<br/><br/>I feel </span>
  <span id="freeText2528624796716828526" style="display:none"><b>“Whatever you do, don't break my brother's heart. You are his world. And if you leave it, it will destroy him.”</b><br /><br /><b>Actual rating: 4.3 out of 5 stars</b><br /><br />The thing about this series is that every book gets better and better and better. I loved 80% of this book so much and enjoyed the other 20% a lot. There's action, romance and a lot of sassy remarks that really does not make this the ideal book to read while on a train because you will start laughing all of a sudden and have people staring at you.<br /><br />I feel like I'm still on a bit of a high from this book and can't form a proper sentence about all the things I loved, so let me just explain to you guys why I didn't give this 5 stars. And I am going to hide that behind a spoiler just in case.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[First, the stuff in the Underworld felt waaaay too simple. It was made out to be a super-difficult thing and possibly either Alex or Aiden would not survive and then it just felt like a walk in the park. A bit disappointing.<br />Second, the fact that Ares was behind all of this was obvious quite early on once they started discussing which god or goddess that could be in charge. Might be because he was a baddie in <i>Percy Jackson</i> as well, or it might be because my sister once wrote a Greek Mythology piece for an English class and had me read it and Ares was the biggest warmonger of all time. So once the first clues showed up I just went "Yep, it's Ares" and then I spent some time being annoyed at the characters not figuring it out as fast as I did. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />And now I'm at that point where I want to read the next (and final) novel, but I'm also terrified that something terrible is going to happen to the Scooby Gang.   <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_328679622" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/328679622" />
    <a title="Erin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4979538-erin"><img alt="Erin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520654483p2/4979538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/328679622?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin" href="/user/show/4979538-erin">Erin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=for-blog-review">for-blog-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=ya-pnr-favorites">ya-pnr-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=autographed-books">autographed-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=arcs-requested">arcs-requested</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer328679622" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1241114412245784029"><br/>Just when I think Jennifer Armentrout has shown us her best and written her most captivating story to date, she goes and ups the ante! I have loved the Covenant series since I first met these incredible characters in the unforgettable Half-Blood, and I thought Deity was just amazing when I read it last year. Well, I can honestly say that, of all Jennifer’s outstanding stories, this is without a doubt her best work to date!!<br/><br/>After reading Deity, I was so anxious and at the same time terribly nervo</span>
  <span id="freeText1241114412245784029" style="display:none"><br>Just when I think Jennifer Armentrout has shown us her best and written her most captivating story to date, she goes and ups the ante! I have loved the Covenant series since I first met these incredible characters in the unforgettable Half-Blood, and I thought Deity was just amazing when I read it last year. Well, I can honestly say that, of all Jennifer’s outstanding stories, this is without a doubt her best work to date!!<br><br>After reading Deity, I was so anxious and at the same time terribly nervous about getting my hands on Apollyon. I knew Aiden and Alex were not in a good place, and I feared there were many dark days ahead that would make for a very painful read. Thankfully, though, this was not the ‘evil possessed Alex’ marathon that I had dreaded. Instead we had an entirely new adventure with our favorite characters, on a quest that had them facing the ghosts of their past and battling each other as well as some downright terrifying creatures. Lucian and Seth are hell-bent on wreaking havoc, and it seems they have help from an unexpected source that is leaning the odds highly in their favor. But in true JLA fashion, balancing out all of the heavy plot twists to perfection is our beloved cast of characters, who had me smiling and snickering right along with them. I’m not sure who was more amusing this time around, Alex or Apollo, but it was a close race!!<br><br><b> Apollo sat back, eyeing the roof of the Hummer like he’d never seen one before. He tapped the internal light once and it flicked on, then he turned it off. Shiny things must be distracting for gods, too. He did it again, brows furrowed. <br>“Apollo,” I snapped. </b><br><br><br><b> “I also doubt Apollo meant for your mouth to be the only thing getting a workout.”-Aiden<br>So many inappropriate comments rose to the tip of my tongue and danced around, but I snapped my jaw shut and glared at him.-Alex </b> <br><br><br>Alex has been my all-time favorite heroine from the moment I began reading this series, but she truly stamps her claim on that title this time around. Always determined and unabashedly brave despite the odds, she is more powerful than ever as an awakened apollyon, and I couldn’t love her more!! We’ve watched Alex go through so much, from the trials of teen angst to enduring torture and the death of loved ones, and through it all she’s been the pillar of strength and kept that spunky outlook that made her so much fun to love! She’s grown right before our eyes into a self-assured, powerful woman who will do anything for those she cares about, even if it means giving up her own life. Yep, she rocks!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380377607i/732971.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And of course, there’s the sexy, brave, and tender Aiden who stole my heart long ago; he had me weak at the knees all over again, and if possible I think I just love him even more!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380377607i/732972._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Apollyon once again showcases JLA’s literary prowess with her breathtaking visuals, engaging characters, and an addicting, captivating plot that was so full of twists and turns that it was nearly impossible to step away. I couldn’t get enough of Aiden and Alex together, and somehow every moment they shared was more beautiful and passionate than the next. In the tales of epic YA love stories, I would say that theirs without a doubt goes down as one of the most breathtaking. Through pain, loss, never-ending obstacles, and even death, their love has survived and flourished to become something unbreakable and unparalleled, and JLA has made it unforgettable!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380377607i/732973._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With danger closing in around them, there was pretty much no way Alex and her crew were going to make it out unscathed. Even if their world didn’t resemble a post-apocalypse thanks to vengeful gods and rampant daimons, something bigger was lurking around the corner, and a huge twist had my stomach in knots and left me feeling ill in it’s aftermath! Ugh, it just tore me to pieces!! Apollyon may be the fourth book of this series, but it packed all the punches of a thrilling debut. It was the perfect blend of gut-wrenching suspense, action, sexy and passionate love story, and fascinating mythological twists, and it had me hooked from start to finish. As much as it will pain me to say goodbye to these characters I love so dearly, I can NOT wait to see the long-awaited conclusion to this phenomenal series when Sentinel releases later this year!!<br><br>Thank you so much to Spencer Hill Press for allowing me to review an ARC of this incredible story!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1241114412245784029" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
