        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1803727196" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14401749934747001880">I swear to God.. If I would have read “My Seth” one more time, I would have hurt someone, mainly Alex!!!!!! “Apollyon” took the series to a whole other level, darker and stronger and you just have a difficult time figuring out your favorite book from the series. It is a very hard task because all of them are amazing and beautifully written, with major events going on and with characters evolving each chapter.<br/><br/>As the title spoils, Alex is the Apollyon now, connected entirely and irevocably with Se</span>
  <span id="freeText14401749934747001880" style="display:none">I swear to God.. If I would have read “My Seth” one more time, I would have hurt someone, mainly Alex!!!!!! “Apollyon” took the series to a whole other level, darker and stronger and you just have a difficult time figuring out your favorite book from the series. It is a very hard task because all of them are amazing and beautifully written, with major events going on and with characters evolving each chapter.<br><br>As the title spoils, Alex is the Apollyon now, connected entirely and irevocably with Seth. The first part of the book was extremely annoying and again, I wanted to punch her in the face for being so blind and stupid!! I had faith that the real Alex will come back to us and Aiden, because Jennifer doesn’t have the heart to torment us long. Things settle at a certain point, but after that everything comes back around and the adventure continues, only this time stronger and more intense. A lot of things will be put together and our team will figure out that they have a greater enemy, with a higher purpose and more dangerous than the “Seth and Lucian” duo.<br><br>“Intense” is the word to describe this book. The events had a more meaningful impact on the readers, the feelings were raw and the way it was transferred to us was overwhelming. There were a lot of parts in the book which I’ve read without breathing. How does Jennifer does it, I don’t know…. But not only without breathing, I was fascinated by the style and the emotion I’ve felt:)<br><br>Speaking of intense, this word can be used to describe Aiden and Alex, because I love them and I know they will stick with me a long time from now on. They took their relationship to a whole different level, and sincerely, I don’t think that “love” is enough to make a proper characterization. What they have is above love and connection, they were amazing and so bonded by a feeling that can’t be described in words. Aiden will be 100% on display now, his feelings out in the open and willing to sacrifice everything for the one he loves. Alex, on the other hand, feels the same, but she will do some mistakes because she is overly protective and such a martyr sometimes. She blames her so much for the hurt or loss of her loved ones, but she will learn to live the moment and fight for everything she believes in.<br><br>I don’t think that I could ever get tired of writing about this series because it is definitely one of the best I’ve read so far.. not only this year, but from always:) I also bought them paperbacks because I just have to get them shinning on my bookshelves. Everything is amazing and dynamic, very well researched and connected. Not all is exposed because Jennifer is giving you pieces to put together, but the outcome is FANTASTIC. I am truly fascinated. Love it:)<br><br>5 stars!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a></span>

<div id="review_438650670" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/438650670" />
    <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library"><img alt="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1350750103p2/4551536.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/438650670?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library">Maja (The Nocturnal Library)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=all-the-right-choices">all-the-right-choices</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=best-of-2013">best-of-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=arc-2013">arc-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=cover-lust">cover-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=my-flat-army">my-flat-army</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=reviewed-in-2013">reviewed-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=just-another-book-crush">just-another-book-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=open-ending">open-ending</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer438650670" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer79662721215917967">By now, it’s pretty clear that Jennifer L. Armentrout knows what she’s doing. Little by little, she’s converted even the strongest non-believers, including me. I still maintain that Half-Blood is a result of blatant plagiarism, but I have changed my mind about the series as a whole, and I’m not one to keep quiet in such an occasion. Ever since Pure, I’ve been enjoying this series more and more with each new installment, and now, with just one book left, I can even call myself a fan. <br/><br/>Deity ended </span>
  <span id="freeText79662721215917967" style="display:none">By now, it’s pretty clear that Jennifer L. Armentrout knows what she’s doing. Little by little, she’s converted even the strongest non-believers, including me. I still maintain that Half-Blood is a result of blatant plagiarism, but I have changed my mind about the series as a whole, and I’m not one to keep quiet in such an occasion. Ever since Pure, I’ve been enjoying this series more and more with each new installment, and now, with just one book left, I can even call myself a fan. <br><br>Deity ended with Alex in the middle of a major disaster. I won’t say much more lest I spoil it for some poor, unsuspecting soul, but it was a vicious cliffhanger – I ranted about it <a href="http://www.thenocturnallibrary.com/2012/12/review-deity-covenant-3.html" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a>. Elixir, the subsequent novella in Aiden’s POV softened the blow just a little bit, but still, Apollyon couldn’t come soon enough. And again, there were no disappointments coming from the JLA camp. Apollyon is just as exciting, just as romantic, just as heartbreaking as the previous installments, if not more. <br><br>Our favorite Sentinels are in the middle of a war. Now that they’re facing a powerful and invisible enemy, Alex’s past problems seem funny in comparison, even to her. The only thing that really keeps her together is that she’s not alone. Although she’s lost so much, she’s still surrounded by her loved ones, both her real family and her replacement family, and she’s willing to do anything to protect them. Now that she’s the Apollyon, she might actually stand a chance, if only she could somehow separate herself from the First and put her own needs first.<br><br>It is almost impossible to predict the outcome in the battle of wills between Alex and Seth. Both are strong, driven, determined to do anything to achieve their goals. But the prophecy says Alex is there to give her power to the First, not the other way around, so defying that prophecy is her only choice.<br><br>Let’s not kid ourselves: we read these books for their plots, and their worldbuilding, and their humor, but above all, we read them for the romance. Let me assure you, the romance in Apollyon is exquisite. Keep those smelling salts within reach, ladies, our favorite couple will make you swoon. <br> <br>Yes, some of Armentrout’s popularity comes from the fact that she doesn’t hesitate to write numerous scenes that are pure fan service, but I’m a fan, and I like to be given exactly what I want. I suppose we could rant about artistic integrity, but honestly, some books you read for their artistic value, and some just to have fun. And guess what? I’m all about fun. So bring it on, JLA! I’ll buy it, I’ll read it, and I’ll thank you for it.<br><br>A huge thank you to Sam @ <a href="http://realmoffiction.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Realm of Fiction</a> for lending me her copy.<br><br><br><a href="http://www.thenocturnallibrary.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380226536i/681142.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="79662721215917967" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer14764316032449104253"><u>Actual Review</u> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781849.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Give me a moment please. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380359586ra/710545.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/387498.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781850.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781851.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781852.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>How can I start but by just simply saying that the long wait was COMPLETELY WORTH IT. SO MUCH.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781853.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>And then there is Aiden and Alex: <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380402311i/781854.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/454844.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781855.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781856.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781857.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/455785.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781858.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781859.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781860.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401850ra/780498.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781861.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380402311ra/781862.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Okay, I'm done. This can't end like that!<br/><br/>I so cannot freaking wait for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13605723.Sentinel__Covenant___5_' title='Sentinel (Covenant, #5) by Jennifer L. Armentrout' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sentinel</a>!<br/><br/>Aiden and Alex didn't have a single moment of peace. Damn! It's time for them to be happy and just love each other freely, without obstacles or worries.<br/><br/>I am just so happy to see Alex changed into a more mature person. She's not as impetuous anymore, which is really great.<br/><br/>After all, she is the Apollyon now. She is very powerful and she can't have those knee-jerk reactions that were so char</span>
  <span id="freeText2740860513037424242" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391864ra/754548.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I swear these authors are trying to kill me. This can't end like that!<br><br>I so cannot freaking wait for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13605723.Sentinel__Covenant___5_" title="Sentinel (Covenant, #5) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Sentinel</a>!<br><br>Aiden and Alex didn't have a single moment of peace. Damn! It's time for them to be happy and just love each other freely, without obstacles or worries.<br><br>I am just so happy to see Alex changed into a more mature person. She's not as impetuous anymore, which is really great.<br><br>After all, she is the Apollyon now. She is very powerful and she can't have those knee-jerk reactions that were so characteristic of her. She needs to be taken seriously and if she was acting like a teenage girl out of control, that wouldn't happen.<br><br>She needs to think very carefully before acting. I hope she can do what has to be done in order to save those she loves and pretty much everybody else.<br><br>Maybe she can even save Seth. In spite of the unforgivable things he has done, I too feel he is not all lost.<br><br>It's so sad he sought love and acceptance in all the wrong places and that he allowed himself to be overpowered by his need for power.<br><br>He is blind to everything outside his own needs and desires. Everything could have been different if he hadn't allowed himself to be molded into someone else's weapon.<br><br>He wouldn't have had what he wanted from Alex, because she loves Aiden, but he would have been happy. He would have had a great friend in Alex and, with time, maybe in Aiden too.<br><br>I can only expect the worse and hope the best.<br><br>But one thing is certain - Alex will never be alone. She has Aiden, always had and will always have. <br><br>Once again, he showed just how incredibly perfect he is.<br><br>I am constantly amazed with the lengths he goes to, in name of his love for Alex. He never gave up on her. He was always the steady light who never flickered.<br><br>I can't possibly imagine how much he suffered seeing everything that was done to his great love, not being able to do anything but fight with everything he got, wait and hope for the best.<br><br>He needs to be happy already. He deserves it! <br><br>*sits in the corner obsessively waiting for Sentinel*<br><br><br><br><br>-----<br>BEFORE READING<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391864ra/754549.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Jennifer, you are trying to kill me!<br>OMG! He is going to take Alex from my Aiden and destroy the freaking world!<br>That cannot be true!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391864ra/754551.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But Alex said that she would never lose herself since she had her love for Aiden and Aiden's love for her.<br>Yes, yes, yes. Calm yourself down, Lucy!</span>

<div id="review_2692509319" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2692509319" />
    <a title="Anja H." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6054186-anja-h"><img alt="Anja H." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559051853p2/6054186.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2692509319?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anja H." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anja H." href="/user/show/6054186-anja-h">Anja H.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2692509319" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3553966097711773335"><b>*4 UPHILL STARS*</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Whatever you do, don't break my brother's heart. You are his world. And if you leave it, it will destroy him.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>HALLELUJAH! </b>This series is <b>finally</b> getting better!<br/>I wanted to give up after the first quarter of this book <s>(I was so frustrated and wanted to repeatedly and agressively bash some characters’ heads in)</s>, but I’m glad I pushed through and now I can’t wait to see what happens in the fifth and final installment!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_256614447" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/256614447" />
    <a title="Annie Brewer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer"><img alt="Annie Brewer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442496062p2/5315988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/256614447?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie Brewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie Brewer" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer">Annie Brewer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=absolutely-amazingly-awesome">absolutely-amazingly-awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=2013-must-have">2013-must-have</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=5-star-worthy">5-star-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=books-on-my-shelf">books-on-my-shelf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=mythology-gods">mythology-gods</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer256614447" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14402869096828377126">Seriously, this series just gets better and better. It surpassed my expectations but of course that's JLA. She can do no fucking wrong! This book was insanely awesome! So much happened and my head was spinning. The action, the romance, the emotions and everything in between. It was just incredible. <br/><br/>Aiden St Delphi is a god of all gods. I fall in love with him more and more and more. Gah! I want him! Team Aiden always.<br/><br/>Review to come closer to release date.<br/><br/>Okay apparently I didn't get the memo tha</span>
  <span id="freeText14402869096828377126" style="display:none">Seriously, this series just gets better and better. It surpassed my expectations but of course that's JLA. She can do no fucking wrong! This book was insanely awesome! So much happened and my head was spinning. The action, the romance, the emotions and everything in between. It was just incredible. <br /><br />Aiden St Delphi is a god of all gods. I fall in love with him more and more and more. Gah! I want him! Team Aiden always.<br /><br />Review to come closer to release date.<br /><br />Okay apparently I didn't get the memo that I can post my review now. Well, it could be that I didn't read the information clearly when I received the book. Anyway, whatever I will get on with this review so I don't bore you all to tears.<br /><br />First of all, A HUGE GRATEFUL THANK YOU to Spencer Hill Press for accepting my request for this ARC!!! I was a basketcase, so happy and ecstatic I cried. Yeah, I'm a baby. Get over it.<br /><br />After I finished Deity, I was a mess. I cried and couldn't believe the end of that book. I'd already been on this huge emotional breakdown throughout the book. It was intense! So when I finished, I was told about the novella from Aiden's (long sigh) POV. I couldn't wait to read that baby. Elixir was by far the best novella I'd read at the time(and now he competes with Ash...and tie). Elixir was so heartbreaking. My emotions were everywhere again. Aiden is just the most genuine, sincere romantic boys out there. And after seeing what he had to do to Alex tore me to pieces because we all knew he hated putting her through that torture. Reading from the guy's POV is emotional and torturous so it was no surprise I found myself crying. Poor Aiden. <br /><br />So when it was finished, I felt slightly satisfied...but still torn and needed Apollyon. So when I put in my request for it, you can imagine the reaction I had when I was told I get it. Ahhhhhhhh, I was so excited! It was like winning the lottery! <br /><br />This will be a hard review to write...I have to keep it spoil free but it's one I have so much to say about. Damn, I guess that is what happens when I get a book ahead of everyone else. So let me keep this semi-short and sweet...before I ramble on and give stuff away. <br /><br />I am having a hard time deciding if I loved Deity or Apollyon better. I think they are tied, BUT I wanna say Apollyon was slightly better. The action was crazy intense...there were so many swoony, steamy moments that made me salivate at the mouth. Oh Aiden, I love that guy!!! Sigh.<br /><br />With that said, each book seems to get better and better. I was hooked instantly. I loved the mythology so much in this book. It was all so fascinating and well done. We get to meet new characters and reunite with old ones that make us smile and some that make us cringe in anger and hatred. The action was so packed, I had whiplash. The romance was to die for. The battle scenes were very well orchestrated and kept you glued to the book, with your heart pumping like crazy.<br /><br />The characters are so amazing! I love Deacon, Marcus, Luke, Lea, Olivia, Alex, Apollo, Solos and of course Aiden. They are all a great group of well-developed characters that made me laugh and root for them during all these crazy scenes. Never a dull moment with Deacon and Luke though. Oh and I still can't stand Seth. That hasn't changed. <br /><br />I know this book is well worth the wait and once you get your hands on it, you won't want to put it down! JLA has outdone herself in this gripping, action packed book, the fourth installment of the Covenant series. A must read!<br /><br />Thanks again to Spencer Hill Press! I will be seething until I get my hands on Sentinel.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14402869096828377126" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_220382124" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/220382124" />
    <a title="~Tina~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2594672-tina"><img alt="~Tina~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411474324p2/2594672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/220382124?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Tina~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Tina~" href="/user/show/2594672-tina">~Tina~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=jennifer-rocks">jennifer-rocks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=own-copy">own-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=read-2013">read-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer220382124" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13779794552485099269">Fanfreakingtastic!!!LOVE LOVE LOVE!!<br/><br/>I swear, I don't know how Jennifer L. Armentrout finds the energy to keep creating amazing books after amazing books. Someone needs to bottle it up and spread it around the world. Think of all the peace we can achieve. But in all seriousness, I've never met a JLA book I didn't like! <br/><br/><b>Apollyon</b> proves to be another exciting installment in the <i>Covenant series</i>, bringing in more action and more romance then ever before, leaving us breathless and begging for the fina</span>
  <span id="freeText13779794552485099269" style="display:none">Fanfreakingtastic!!!LOVE LOVE LOVE!!<br><br>I swear, I don't know how Jennifer L. Armentrout finds the energy to keep creating amazing books after amazing books. Someone needs to bottle it up and spread it around the world. Think of all the peace we can achieve. But in all seriousness, I've never met a JLA book I didn't like! <br><br><b>Apollyon</b> proves to be another exciting installment in the <i>Covenant series</i>, bringing in more action and more romance then ever before, leaving us breathless and begging for the final conclusion.<br><br>I gotta tell ya, some of the hardest reviews I have to write are the ones that have to be spoil-free and the ones that I'm most passionate and excited about. Which are usually all of JLA books.<br>I always find myself struggling with the right words to convey how much I adored this book and this series, but without giving away to much. I am just such a fan of everything this women puts to pen and in complete awe of her never ending imagination and creativity. She plots in her evil mad genius ways and is an unflinching force when it comes to writing these remarkable characters. <br><br>There is a lot that happens in this book, but not all of our questions were answered. The biggest questions are still to come for the last hurrah. Almost like Jennifer gave us yummy appetizers to sink our teeth into before the main course is revealed. And the best part? We aren't left hanging with our mouths open gasping for air. Evil cliffy be gone! <br>Plot wise, everything gets stepped up a notch. Everyone is running around doing damage control and grasping at straws to figure out how to stop the First from destroying the entire world while trying to tame the Gods long enough for Alex to come out of the dark side and join the side of the sane. All the while Aiden is festering with guilt for putting Alex through one of her greatest fears. So in short, lot of drama, lots of angst and lot and lots of swoon worthy goodness all for our reading pleasure.<br>The mythology also takes a front seat in this book even more so then the previous ones. We get to see some new Godly faces and one of them shocked the Hades out of me! I've always been a huge fan of mythology and love the way Jennifer handles this lore. It's fun and unpredictable and it constantly keeps me on my toes. <br><br>All the characters are just so amazing. Some seemed to grow in new and different ways. The atmosphere is more dangerous and dire and it's like they can taste it in the air. They are all preparing for the best but also expecting the worse. For Seth fans, he's in this book...but he's not at the same time. And for Aiden fans, well, the man just keeps getting better and sweeter then ever. It's amazing to witness his playful and feisty side opposed to his ever present stubbornness and control. I laughed out loud at his protectiveness in this book considering who and what Alex is. So adorable!<br>Alex has always awed me, she's such an incredible protag and the perfect character to go on this journey<br>with. Her laid back personality and sarcastic charm mixed with her kickass abilities is nothing short of brilliance.<br>We also get to see an old friend that leaves a warm fuzzy feeling in my heart. Those scenes really add<br>beautifully to the story line.<br>As for the romance, well, lets just say those were my favorite moments and I gave each scene an extra read three or five times before moving on. It was just so dame sweet and curl-your-toes romantic that I couldn't get the stupid-grin off my face. Loved will never be a strong enough word.<br>And last but not least, the ending might not have ended on a cliffhanger, but it was a different kind of brutal that was very hard to read. And that's all I'm gonna say about that.<br><br>Bottom line, with the risk of sounding like a broken record on repeat, I absolutely loved this book. The Convent series is one of the most addicting and heart pounding books I ever read. It's fun and funny and I always find myself bouncing with pure joy when ever I get a chance to read these books early and end up with the hugest grin on my face and a big pit of worry in my belly when it's all said and done.<br>This is the stuff that makes reading, magic!<br><br>Action punched and pulse pounding madness. Apollyon is the forth installment in the covenant series and the best one to date. It will have you on your knees begging for the final book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13605723.Sentinel__Covenant___5_" title="Sentinel (Covenant, #5) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Sentinel</a>!!<br><br>(Arc provided by Spencer Hill Press in exchange for an honest review)<br><br>This review and more can be seen at WinterHaven Books;<br><br><a href="http://www.winterhavenbooks.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380333076i/693179.png" alt="winter haven books" width="150" height="111" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13779794552485099269" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Daniella (Reading With Daniella)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella"><img alt="Daniella (Reading With Daniella)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1501986323p2/41915343.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1738798387?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Daniella (Reading With Daniella)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Daniella (Reading With Daniella)" href="/user/show/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella">Daniella (Reading With Daniella)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=read-free-online">read-free-online</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=ya-fantasy-dystopian-sci-fi">ya-fantasy-dystopian-sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=read-more-than-once">read-more-than-once</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1738798387" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18115959892395299268"><a href='https://readingwithdaniella.wordpress.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Click here to see this review and others on my blog Reading With Daniella</a><br/><br/><b> July 2017: </b>I'm beginning think that my amount of love for Jennifer Armentrout and this series is getting dangerously out of control. <br/><br/>I don't even have the words to describe how incredible this was. This series just keeps getting better and better, totally exceeding my expectation and blowing me way entirely. <br/>The story was just bursting with love, bad-assery, character growth, super awesome relationships, shocking plot twis</span>
  <span id="freeText18115959892395299268" style="display:none"><a href="https://readingwithdaniella.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Click here to see this review and others on my blog Reading With Daniella</a><br /><br /><b> July 2017: </b>I'm beginning think that my amount of love for Jennifer Armentrout and this series is getting dangerously out of control. <br /><br />I don't even have the words to describe how incredible this was. This series just keeps getting better and better, totally exceeding my expectation and blowing me way entirely. <br />The story was just bursting with love, bad-assery, character growth, super awesome relationships, shocking plot twists, cool gods, and every other brilliant thing I could ever hope for. <br />The ending was absolutely phenomenal, and I'm pretty sue I held my breath for the entire last few pages. It was SO intense!<br /><br />Aiden was hotter and sweeter than ever, which I did not even realize was possible, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ though the part with his guilt about the brew drove me insane! I felt so bad for Alex because he was avoiding her when she needed him most, but I also felt bad for Aiden because he felt so unnecessarily guilty. It just tore my heart out. Also, he never once gave up on Alex when she was connected to Seth, and always saw the girl that he loved was somewhere, buried deep within her. It was beautiful to see how lovingly persistent he was, especially when he finally got through to her. He was so careful to never even lay a finger on her when she was coming close to killing him in the outside of the cabin. Now that is love!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br />Deacon was even more hilarious than ever, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ and I adored seeing a few peeks at his relationship with Luke.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br />Apollo was also absolutely hilarious and I have come to love his character so much!<br />And of course, Alex was as sassy and kickass as ever. She also went under a lot of growth and development throughout the book, and her relationship with Marcus really grew, which I loved. I think that he's a great uncle and he really cares about her, but he just doesn't know how to show it. Especially in the first book, where I hate him. It's kind of funny to look back on that now because each of the characters have come so far from where they started and I feel so proud. <br /><br />If you haven't read this series yet, I would highly suggest doing so! It is beyond words.<br /><br /><b>March 2019: </b> Listening to this as an audio book makes some of the lines seem sooo cheesy! Also, what is up with all of the characters pressing their foreheads together all. the. time? Do people actually do this? Because the characters in practically every single one of her books do. And it's weird.<br /><br />I also just noticed how much I like the synopsis of this book. I love the opening line: <i>"Fate isn't something to mess with and now, neither is Alex."</i> It perfectly captures the theme of the story!</span>
  <a data-text-id="18115959892395299268" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MQJEkb3MaNW12Iu2hb30NU6PUUIGqOGVHjOEXcyYAaULJC1DBpKhvRLzP9dySP7qmNC2isglb/JFTcLsAdvzPw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9yHRZarFnc+qkacCgSvpHpdA7EDHYIn+9LPagOZ1iPbNB7i3EZtUpw26E2N23uPBQR8LiAntB5mvzZwxKzZ6bA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText6695982593142102039" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
